NOVEMBER 22, 1980, DEDHAM MASSACHUSETTS

You lie in your bed, taking shallow breaths. You’ve felt it coming for days, and you’re sure that today will be your last day among the living.

You lay quietly, reflecting on the many years behind you. Across the room, a few newspaper clippings are pinned to a board. “McCormack Elevated to the Presidency, Johnson Resigns!” reads one. “Goldwater Elected President. McCormack prepares for Transition of Power” reads another. A more recent clipping from a Magazine sticks out: “John McCormack: The Great Caretaker and Last Real Leader of Our Time.”

You wonder where the author is now. It’s been years since the press was allowed to write anything so provocative. You can’t remember when, but slowly, thanks to the current “administration,” freedom of speech and freedom of the press has eroded, slowly and steadily.

The Administration in question just got re-elected for its third term. The Devil and his lapdog were back in Washington once again, planning their next four years of slowly dismantling the constitution, and the nation you devoted your life to. You’d had your nurse send in your mail-in vote, and you’d heard Massachusetts was one of the few states McCarthy might actually win, but you knew it was a sham. The disease and rot the devil brought with him to Washington was simply too deep now, and a simple election wouldn’t be enough to undo it. No doubt his lackeys had corrupted the sacred process of voting, too.

As you lay back, taking your final few breaths, you close your eyes and let the darkness take you. What you couldn’t know, was that miles away, the lapdog you had always pitied was in Washington, and he was about to stumble on something far darker and far sinister than you could possibly imagine.

As the reaper takes you, you leave the darkness of the nation you’d once loved behind you. But as you depart, you see, for a fleeting moment, a spark of light on the horizon.

" }else if (campaignTrail_temp.player_answers[17] == 18001 && aa[0].electoral_votes == 269 && aa[1].electoral_votes == 269) { used=false if (used != true) { setInterval(function () { used = true; imgg = document.getElementsByClassName("person_image")[0]; if (imgg != null) { imgg.src = "https://i.imgur.com/7sQAIIT.png"; } }, 100); } return "

ELECTION DEADLOCKED! MCCORMACK INVITED TO BECOME VP IF HOUSE CANNOT MAKE DECISION BY JANUARY!

Well, this wasn’t exactly how things were meant to go, was it?

Already, you were never meant to be President, and here you are overseeing the second deadlocked election in Presidential history.

The weeks since election day have almost been more chaotic than the unprecedented campaign behind you. The Electoral College, of course, deadlocked, and what ensued was a vicious tug of war between the parties.

First, they tried striking a deal, but that went nowhere fast. Then, they tried to let congress decide - some good that did them. While the Senate, which remained narrowly Democratic, already selected the Vice President of their ticket, the house was not so simple. Due to Goldwater’s unprecedented gains, and poor turnout, the House is also delegated, with 25 Democratic delegations, and 25 Republican ones.
